Yangtze River Rises Over Twenty Feet 63

Hankou Dispatch: The water level of the Yangtze River's upper reaches has risen sharply by more than twenty feet in the past ten days. The rapid current flows eastward, and the waves are turbulent. Tragic boat capsizing incidents on the Wuhan river surface are a daily occurrence. The small ferries traveling between Wuhan and Jing, loaded with passengers, were heading towards the pontoons of the Jianghanguan Customs around 5:00 PM the day before yesterday. As they were about to dock, they were suddenly hit by a wave and turned towards the center of the river. A small steamer from behind was also deflected by the force of the water. The helmsman was unable to control it, and it slammed into the ferry. The ferry's stern was torn apart, and river water entered through the windows. The boat gradually began to sink. Fortunately, more than a hundred boats along the riverbank rushed forward to rescue the passengers on board, and a tugboat towed the ferry into the factory, saving hundreds of passengers from the tragedy of drowning. Unexpectedly, around 9:00 PM on the 28th, the Wu'an commercial steamer, while sailing near the Jianghanguan Customs, turned its rudder carelessly due to the surging river waves and crashed into the Jardine Matheson pontoon. The boiler exploded, and the fire compartment was shattered. The ship immediately sank, and all the workers and staff on board, more than ten people, were drowned. Because there are no ferries on the beaches of Parrot Island and Baisha Island, merchants and civilians crossing the river must take rowboats. At 1:00 PM on the 29th, a small rowboat carrying three passengers was heading upstream from Baisha Island when it was overturned by the angry waves in the middle of the river. The passengers and boatman were all drowned. Moreover, the river water has been rising continuously for days. According to some people, the sudden rise in river water this time is reddish in color, indicating a major flood in Sichuan. The rising trend is just beginning. Fang Dazhi, the Director of the Hubei Water Conservancy Bureau, fearing that the embankments along the river will be in danger, has recently sent out eighty flood prevention personnel, led by engineers, carrying funds to inspect and repair the embankments in various counties along the river. In areas where bandits and communists have not been cleared, a request has been submitted to the General Headquarters to dispatch troops for protection. (June 30th)

Hangzhou Quick Dispatch 64

The implementation of the Zhejiang Province straw hat donation and merchant-recognized office, originally scheduled for July 1st, has been postponed by order of the Department of Finance due to insufficient preparation. The long-distance telephone lines in Wenling and Changshan, Zhejiang Province, have been completed and are now open for calls. Staff are currently being dispatched to set up branch offices.

The joint transportation method of the Provincial Highway Bureau's Hang-Mo (Hangzhou-Moganshan) bus service and the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway began yesterday. The bus departs from the City Station for Moganshan at 2:15 PM every day. The yarn merchants from the six counties under Jiaxing Prefecture, feeling that the increased tax rate after the Department of Finance took back the official operation of the yarn donation was unbearable, specially sent representatives to Hangzhou to petition the provincial government and the Department of Finance to reduce the donation rate to the same level as Jiangsu Province, but have not yet obtained a response. The Department of Construction ordered the Navigation Bureau to take over the inland navigation business of the China Merchants Bureau. Chen Yi has been appointed as the director of the Zhejiang Provincial Navigation Bureau's Inland Steamship Business Office, concurrently serving as the general manager of the China Merchants Bureau's Inland Steamship Bureau. Yesterday, he, along with Hong Jiayi and Shu Zhendong, technicians from the Department of Construction, went to Shanghai and then to Jiahu and other areas to take over.

Chao-Mei Bandit News 65

Various counties urgently hope for military officers to advance and suppress. Xiang Hanping plans to inspect various counties. Shantou Dispatch: In various counties of Chaozhou and Meizhou, the local communists are rampant, ravaging the local people, who are living in dire straits. For example, on the 12th, the local bandits in Fengshun County captured Jiuhe Township, Luohuang District. All the men, women, old, and young in the township fled. Several able-bodied men were captured, doused with kerosene, and burned alive. Such inhumanity is commonplace. Others who could not escape were either scalded with boiling water or beaten to death with thorny sticks. On the 23rd, taking advantage of the transfer of the Luohuang garrison, the bandits attacked Luohuang, whose guards were outnumbered and unable to resist. Luohuang was captured and two Luohuang public schools and five or six shops were burned, and there was extensive looting. On the 24th, Chen Ju's regiment sent a battalion, together with the Special Task Battalion of Huang Hanlin's unit from Chaoan, to drive away the local communists. Luohuang is the fourth district of Fengshun and a commercial port on the right bank of the Han River. A company of guards is stationed in Huangjin City, Baitou, Huangdong, and Wei Township. Although there are local militias, their strength is very weak and they cannot compete with the bandits. When Luohuang was captured on the 23rd, the communist bandits distributed leaflets in Dasha Keng, Baitou Township, Fengliu Men, and Gaosha Township. The bandits led by Pan Tianji and She Huangji were also very active, ambushing and killing more than forty merchants carrying goods on their shoulders at Baifenpu Xikengping. All the goods were looted. The main force of the communist bandits, led by Li Mingguang, set up a headquarters in Baixi, proclaiming that they would seize Luohuang Huangjin City within ten days and cut off Han River traffic. Since the 23rd, the ferries up and down the Han River have been suspended due to the bandits. Moreover, above Luohuang, in Shigou and Chanxi, local communists are gathering to loot civilian boats. Boatmen must form gangs and hire merchant guards to escort them before daring to pass. The newly appointed magistrate of Fengshun County, He Naiying, specially requested 6,000 rounds of ammunition from the 62nd Division and brought them with him to take office. The difficulty of being the magistrate of Fengshun County can be imagined. Dabuzhen County, which is adjacent to Fengshun, has several hundred communist bandits holding up the red flag of the Dabuzhen Revolutionary Committee Military Affairs Committee Special Task Force. On the 22nd, they invaded Dangxi and engaged in a battle at Yintan Aoshan with the police force of Guo Hanyuan, the director of the Dama United Defense. The police force killed more than ten bandits, and the bandits retreated to the Fujian border. Currently, the local communists in various districts of the county are still carrying out large-scale activities. The following is the text of the joint telegram from various Dabuzhen County agencies requesting troops: "We humbly report that Dabuzhen County is surrounded by bandit territory. In recent months, those who have been ravaged by bandits account for seven or eight out of ten. For example, Shiyun, Dabu Corner, Baihou, Dashen, Nanshan in Pudong, Zaicheng, Changzhi, Zhangxi, Yanshang in Pubei, Dama, Yinjiang, Dangxi in Puxi, Gaobei, Chishui, Sanzhou, and Taohua in Punan have been successively lost, burned, and killed. The situation is extremely tragic. Although the defense forces have carried out suppression operations one after another, they cannot suppress this fleeing. The transfer of troops loses protection, and the police teams in various districts are weak. The people have fled, the commercial market is closed, and the citizens are cut off. Representatives have witnessed the tragedy and crawl to Shantou to humbly request the dispatch of troops to divide and defend and suppress the bandits on behalf of the 300,000 souls of the entire county." Furthermore, Xingning, Wuhua, and Meixian, which are adjacent to the northern border of Fengshun, have also been greatly disturbed by communist bandits. Anliu, Meilin, Shuangtou, Shangxiaba, and Shangshan eight villages in Wuhua County have long been under the control of the communist bandit Gu Dacun. In Meixian, the villages of Shekeng, Shuiche, Guantang, Xintang, and Changsha in the upper reaches of the Mei River are often harassed by bandits who block the river and rob ships, obstructing the waterway. Recently, bandits stationed in Shekengxu and waved red flags across the river. Gu Dacun invaded Xingning Zoudong on the 19th but was defeated by the local militia there. On the 21st, he again gathered more than a thousand local communists from Jiulongzhang on the Meifeng border and attacked Xingning Putou Dam Shuikou Shekeng police team at dawn. The police team rose up to rescue them. The battle continued until the afternoon. Zhang Ying's camp of the Xingning garrison and a company of government troops stationed in Dili Xiang crossed the river from Shekeng and attacked Gu Dacun's rear. The local communists were attacked from both sides and collapsed towards Fozigao, Xiaosang, and other places in the evening. The military police cooperated to pursue and suppress them, killing more than a hundred bandits and seizing a large number of reactionary publications and military supplies. They pursued them for more than thirty li before returning. Currently, Gu Dacun has retreated to Xiashe Maokeng Songkeng and other places. Various counties are eagerly awaiting the government troops to launch a large-scale suppression and have repeatedly sent representatives to Shantou to request troops from Xiang Hanping, commander of the 63rd Division. It is heard that Xiang plans to inspect various counties during the day and transfer Luo Weiying's unit, which is returning to the province from Wuzhou, to Chaozhou and Shantou to assist in defense. He will also transfer Luo Xiuli's supplementary regiment from Zhaoqing to garrison Huizhou, Hailufeng, and other counties. After returning to Shantou from the inspection, he may plan to encircle and suppress the communist bandits. (June 26th) Local Communications

Songjiang 67

The County's Organizing Committee Propaganda Department held a grand meeting at the County Party Department Auditorium at 9:00 AM yesterday to celebrate the 5th anniversary of the establishment of the National Government. About 100 representatives from all walks of life attended the ceremony. The Fengjing robbery and murder case was reported yesterday. It is now known that the victim of the robbery and murder case in Fengjing Fenwutou, map 26, was a farmer named Hua Jinxian, who lived in Hujia with his elderly father, Hua Yinquan. They made a living by farming and had no savings. Around 9:00 PM on the 20th day of the lunar May, more than ten bandits broke into the small house and beat them. They tied up Yinquan and his son and demanded silver dollars. When they failed to get them, they beat them severely. Finally, they gave them forty silver dollars. The bandits were still not satisfied and set a date for them to pay a certain amount again on the 28th at the South Railway Station in Shanghai. Only after this agreement was reached were they released. After robbing the farmer, they lost a lot of money, and they really couldn't raise the money for the agreed-upon payment. The bandits, seeing that they hadn't come by the deadline, broke into the house around 10:00 PM on the 28th of last month. Hua Jinxian had just unlocked the door when he was shot and killed by the bandits. The bandits left after their goal had been achieved. The old father was extremely saddened by the sight and almost fainted. He reported the incident to the authorities the next day. It is now known that the county government has sent Secretary Zhang Shengwu to investigate and has immediately ordered the water and land police under its jurisdiction to strictly investigate and arrest the perpetrators.

Jiading 69

The Education Bureau Passes the Annual Salary Increase. The County Education Bureau held its fourth education administrative meeting on the 29th of last month and passed the long-pending annual salary increase for primary schools. The agreed-upon methods are as follows: Those who have continued to work in the county for three years will receive a one-level increase, those who have worked for six years will receive a two-level increase, those who have worked for eight to fourteen years will receive a one-level increase every two years, and those who have worked for fifteen to eighteen years will receive a one-level increase every year. Each level will receive an annual salary increase of twenty-four yuan, but there is a maximum limit. The highest monthly salary for central school principals is sixty-five yuan, the highest monthly salary for central directors and senior homeroom teachers of full primary schools is forty-five yuan, the highest monthly salary for single-grade primary school principals is forty-two yuan, the highest monthly salary for junior primary school principals and homeroom teachers and senior primary school subject teachers is forty yuan, and the highest monthly salary for junior primary school subject teachers is thirty-five yuan. Other specific grade increases can be added outside the limit.

Wuxi 71

Reactions to Road Widening. Yao Dixing, the Director of the Wuxi County Construction Bureau and the Director of the Municipal Engineering Office, believes that the streets in the urban area are unusually narrow and uneven. Therefore, he decided to widen Sanxiatang Zhijie first, in two steps. The first step is to widen the road to six meters (approximately 20 feet) at once. The second step will be to widen it to nine meters (approximately 30 feet). If the houses in the area need to be rebuilt, they will be gradually widened according to this standard to facilitate traffic. He had already sent personnel to survey and prepare a plan to be submitted to the Department of Construction for approval. Unexpectedly, Tao Guanshi, the town head of the Central District, and Qian Baohua, a citizen, took the initiative to oppose it and submitted a request to the Construction Bureau to withdraw the people's lives. Yesterday, local elders Hua Yisan, Yang Changyuan, Wei Zhiwen, and others gathered 34 people and jointly submitted a request to the Construction Bureau to comply with the people's wishes and stipulate that all houses along Sanxiatang be widened to 20 feet when they are rebuilt and gradually reach full completion over a number of years. Director Yao, after receiving the request, stated that since the road widening plan had been submitted to the Department of Construction for approval, he should wait for the department's approval to handle it.

The verdict in the Miao Bin extortion case. Street ruffians Deng Asan, Lü Yulian, and Hang Bingkui sent letters to extort Miao Bin, the former Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Civil Affairs. The Water and Land Police Team, disguised, designed to arrest the above-mentioned criminals one after another. After being taken to the bureau, they were transferred to the county for research. All three confessed to the extortion case. Realizing that there was no way out, Hang Bingkui's parents kowtowed to Mrs. Miao, requesting that she find a way to forgive and spare their ignorance. Yesterday, Magistrate Sun signed and brought the three criminals Deng, Lü, and Hang to be re-tried. He instructed them in court that they should all be sentenced to death for the crimes they had committed, but they were leniently treated due to their ignorance and were each sentenced to two years of imprisonment for attempted extortion.

The prime suspect in the joint robbery of the Yinan Tax Card was arrested. On March 25th, at 6:00 PM, the Julongqiao branch of the Yinan Tax Office was robbed by bandits. The water police guarding the card and 236 yuan and 56 cents in tax funds, as well as 353 yuan in private funds from the employees, and 1,300 yuan from a freight friend named Wang Daoduan who was staying overnight at the branch, were all robbed. After the incident, Wang Youlong, the director of the office, reported to Wang Chengguo, the captain of the 9th team of the 2nd District of the Water Police stationed at the card, who successively arrested Shao Jinsheng and six others, who confessed that the bandit leader was named Song Xidu, who had committed numerous crimes and had now fled without a trace. Yesterday, Ni Gusheng, the captain of the Detective Team of the 2nd District of the Water Police stationed in Wuxi, learned that the bandit leader Song Xidu was hiding in Henglin. He immediately led the detectives to the station, where Song was about to board a train to escape. He immediately reported to the station's military police, who cooperated to capture Song and temporarily escorted him to the military police company headquarters in preparation for his return to Yixing for interrogation.

The opening date of the Xicheng Highway. Since the Construction Bureau actively worked on the Xicheng Highway, the entire road project was 80-90% complete by the end of last month. Only Bridge No. 7 in Yanqiao Town still needs to be paved. At the latest, the entire road will be completed within half a month. The Construction Bureau has decided to hold a completion and opening ceremony for the entire road at the end of this month.

Jiangyin 72

Detained a suspect in the Shanghai massacre of seven lives. Yang Bingwei of the Public Security Bureau's Detective Team reported that Han Bingsheng and Sun Heshang's house in Lujia Garden in the city had three suspicious people who spoke with a Shanghai accent, Zhu Tingyu, Zhu Ronggui, and Xiao Yunjun, who were suspected of being involved in the massacre of seven lives at Guo Chunsen's home on Aiwanyi Road to Delhi in Shanghai on April 25th. Captain Yang led the team to Sun Heshang's house in the garden in the afternoon and arrested Zhu Tingyu and the other two. They searched the house and found many leather bags, foot baskets, and silk clothes, as well as Buddhist books, women's clothing, half-length photos of a man dressed as a woman, and photos taken with an old woman and an old nun in Hangzhou. They took them to the team headquarters for interrogation. According to Zhu Tingyu, he was 24 years old, originally lived in Yaojiawan, Dadongmen, Shanghai, and now lives in Sanlintang, Pudong. He opened the Yifeng Wood Firm in Dongjiadu. His manager was Hong Baosheng. His father's name was Zhu Shaoqi, who was retired in Hong Kong and had previously served as the director of the Jiujiang Police Department. He left home with his stepmother in March of this year. Zhu Ronggui was from Chuansha Dongwai and came to his home last winter as a servant. Xiao Yunjun was his fellow apprentice and was a plasterer from Jinqiao, Jiangyin. After the three of them came to Cheng, they lived in the house of his adoptive mother, Han Naisheng. His words had nothing to do with the Guo case. After comparing them with the photo of Guo Songan published in the Shanghai newspaper on April 27th, they did not look alike. However, his story was bizarre. He had been in Jiangyin for more than two months, never leaving the house all day. He lived extravagantly, was a vegetarian, and recited the Buddha's name. He burned tin foil Guanyin scriptures and the Great Compassion Mantra every day. Zhu and Xiao claimed to be servants. The villagers in the garden called Tingyu the Fourth Young Master. There was also a servant-like person living there on May 28th, but she disappeared yesterday. It is difficult to determine whether Zhu Tingyu is his real name. In the evening, he was sent to the headquarters for further interrogation, but he did not provide any definite information and his words were contradictory. It is worth studying. Zhu Tingyu claimed that there was an accountant named Kang Shuitian living on Ningbo Road, who could collect 20,000 yuan in rent every month. Today (the 1st), Detective Team members He Atong and Wu Shanbao were ordered to go to Shanghai for detailed investigation before verifying the matter.

Zhenjiang 73

The county magistrate's office expenses will still be paid as before. The former Jiangsu Provincial Government, in order to implement austerity measures, intended to remove the item of office expenses for county magistrates from the budget for the 19th year. However, Hu, the director of the Department of Civil Affairs, believed that the duties of county magistrates were very heavy. If this office expense was removed, virtuous officials would face the risk of personal losses due to public affairs, while unscrupulous officials would be tempted to seek illegal compensation. The desire for transparency would be hindered. Moreover, the total amount of this office expense for the whole year was only about 160,000 to 170,000 yuan, which was not much for the provincial treasury to spend, but the impact on the future of administration would be significant. Therefore, he specially requested the provincial government to continue to provide it in order to encourage integrity. The provincial government has already passed it in a meeting.

The education community in Taicang came to the province to petition. People from the education community in Taicang believed that the director of the county's education bureau regarded the education bureau as his own, disregarding public opinion and harboring private intentions, so that education was not progressing. Yesterday, they specially sent representatives to the province and prepared a petition to the provincial government, listing the director's various illegal activities. They came to the provincial government to petition, sincerely requesting that the director be dismissed. There was a great tendency to not stop until their goal was achieved. The Department of Education has already sent personnel to investigate.

Young Man Named Chen Commits Suicide by Jumping into the Sea A certain steamship sailing from Ningbo to Shenjiamen asked [unclear]. A young passenger with a long face and a flat head, about 20 years old, speaking in the Fenghua dialect, wearing a gray silk long gown and a flat-topped straw hat, had no luggage. When the ship sailed outside Zhenhai Port at 10:15 a.m., he walked to the left side of the ship to urinate. Unexpectedly, he suddenly jumped into the sea and committed suicide. The sailors noticed it and reported it to the captain, who turned the rudder to rescue him, but there was no sign of him. Only the straw hat was slightly submerged and immediately swept away by the waves. The tea room found a suicide note in the cabin. The cover only read "Fenghua Person Chen" and the numbers "June 27, 19th Year".

Compilation of Bandit Troubles in Yinxi There is a woman named Liang in Yinschen Bridge, whose husband died early, leaving behind a son who is studying in a certain elementary school. The family is still wealthy and hires workers to plant rice fields, while the woman wanders in the fields. When asked, it was revealed that she was kidnapped by bandits earlier this month. Now both parties have agreed to pay 1,050 yuan to redeem her. Also, Qian Kuikui of the Xiejiatang Seawall Wangjia in Baigong had a small fortune. At midnight last year, his only son, Jia, was suddenly kidnapped by bandits, who demanded a huge ransom. After several contacts, there was no clue. It was not until the day before yesterday that the conditions were negotiated, and 3,600 yuan was paid to redeem his son at Huangniling outside the South Gate of Yuyao. Also, at about 12:00 the night before last, bandits came from Sanxikou to Tongxiantang Pharmacy in Shipoqiao Street, Fengting Township, 15 miles away from Yuyao City, as well as the hotel opened by the Chen widow of Xintaixiang Grocery Store. They were armed with wooden [unclear] and flashlights, wearing yellow shorts and sneakers. They first broke into Tongxiantang and robbed them with weapons, causing a loss of about 160 yuan. After Tongxiantang was robbed, they entered the widow Chen's house and robbed them again, causing a total loss of more than 100 yuan. Finally, they went to Xintaixiang Foreign Goods Store to rob them wantonly. When Zhao Huisheng, the manager of the store, heard the news, he prepared to defend, but unexpectedly, the opportunity was not secret, and he was spotted by the bandits, who tied Zhao to the pillar and demanded 1,000 yuan in cash, and beat him with objects, causing him considerable injuries. The total loss is estimated to be more than 300 yuan.

Huzhou 80

Poisonous Mushrooms Harm People In the mountainous villages of Huzhou, after every moldy rain, a kind of yellow mushroom grows in the rotten grass, which the villagers call cogongrass mushroom or green seedling mushroom. They pick it and cook it, and its taste is quite delicious. This kind of mushroom is most common in the mountains of the western villages. On the 28th of this month, Pan Chunwu from Miaoxizhen near the southwest village of Wuxing picked half a small basket of mushrooms. After cooking them, eight members of the family, except for worker Yu A'er, who did not eat them due to a foot disease, all had severe abdominal pain in less than half an hour. Fortunately, a neighbor knew it was mushroom poison and immediately bought two flavors of Jinzhi Xiangjun and fried them together. The patients took one bowl each, and after one hour, they all vomited and had diarrhea several times, and the abdominal pain stopped. Only then were they all well.

Hangzhou-Changxing Buses Also Carry Packages Since the opening of the Hangzhou-Changxing bus, business has been developing daily, so the Provincial Highway Bureau has decided to also operate the business of transporting packages from July 1 in order to further facilitate matters. All mail, packages, and other clothing and packages of private individuals or agencies and organizations can be transported on their behalf.

Shangyu 81

The Case of a Party Member Assaulting and Insulting Another Party Member Has Been Judged Chen Haoyang and Wu Jiongwei, members of the First Branch of the Second District, were sentenced for assaulting and insulting Zhu Guangyao, a resident of Hutangxia, on the road this spring due to a long-standing dispute over fish ponds. The county government has recently sentenced Chen Haoyang to seven months in prison for encroachment and assault, and Wu Jiongwei has been granted probation and bail. Zhejiang Chunhui Middle School, which was Robbed by Bandits Zhejiang Chunhui Middle School in Shangyu was suddenly robbed by bandits on the 10th of this month, and Principal Fan Shoukang, teachers Wu Minxing, and student Xia Dingcai were kidnapped. The details have been repeatedly recorded in this newspaper. Now it is known that the school board of the middle school decided to suspend the school temporarily because the school was robbed and the people were panicked, and submitted a report to the Department of Education for filing. The Department of Education replied yesterday, saying that the school's sudden robbery was an extraordinary event, and that the whole school was panicked. However, a school that is known for its achievements should not be shut down, which would not only violate the original intention of the school board to educate talents, but also affect the academic future of hundreds of students. The school board has worked hard in the past and should continue to maintain and improve the school to create future talents. Furthermore, after the school board decided to suspend the school, the students were deeply opposed to it, so they organized a school protection movement committee to call on all sectors of society for assistance, sent letters to all school board members to encourage them to maintain the school, and sent representatives Zhu Huancai, Luo Jieren, and Zhang Shijun on the 22nd to request assistance from various agencies. County Magistrate Chen, Education Bureau Director Che, and the secretary of the County Party Department all met with them and believed that it was very inappropriate to close Chunhui Middle School, which has a history in Zhejiang Province, due to the robbery. Therefore, they expressed their sympathy for the school protection movement committee organized by Chunhui students and planned to immediately call on the provincial government's Department of Education to find ways to maintain it. On the 24th, representatives Luo Jieren, Tao Siqi, Luo Wenhua, and Zhu Huancai went to Hengshan to meet with the school owner, Chen Qiushan, but were unable to meet him. Later, they went to the school board member Chen Yizhai's place to state their intentions and appeal to the advantages and disadvantages of suspending the school in Hui, and the suffering of more than 400 students who were struggling to find education. School Board Member Chen expressed his sympathy, but a definite solution would have to wait until the next school board meeting to decide. Letter from

Ministry of Education

Strictly Prohibits the Display of Religious Books and Newspapers 84

The Ministry of Education strictly prohibits church schools from displaying religious books and pictures in their libraries. In addition to informing the Propaganda Department of the Central Executive Committee, it also issued a notice to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities, stating that the Propaganda Department of the Central Executive Committee sent an official letter stating that the propaganda department of the Wuxian Party Affairs Consolidation Committee reported that the display of religious books and newspapers in the libraries of church schools in various places is an imperialist tool to promote aggression through cultural propaganda and to anesthetize the minds of young people. It requested strict prohibition to prevent future troubles. The Ministry found that the display of religious books, newspapers, and pictures in the libraries of church schools in order to anesthetize the minds of young people should be strictly prohibited. From now on, all schools should prohibit the display or hanging of all religious propaganda pictures. With regard to religious books, newspapers, and magazines, except for those related to elective subjects and very [unclear] philosophical references in universities and senior high schools, the rest should be [unclear] prohibited. In addition to issuing orders, it is ordered to comply and transfer them for compliance.

Postage for Books Could Not Be Reduced 85

The case of the Chinese Library Association requesting a reduction in postage for sending books was deemed by the Executive Yuan to be difficult to implement after deliberation by the Department of Transportation. Recently, the Secretariat of the Executive Yuan sent a letter to the Ministry of Education, stating that the Transportation Department's reply to the Chinese Library Association's resolution to reduce postage for sending books from libraries was submitted by the President of the Executive Yuan for review. After detailed review, it was deemed difficult to implement. The order was given to the Ministry of Education, etc. for reference. The original letter stated that the Executive Yuan ordered the Ministry of Education to submit the five opinions of the first annual meeting resolution of the Executive Committee of the Chinese Library Association for review. An order was given to reduce the postage for review and reply. Copies of the original letter of the association and the opinions of the Ministry of Education were issued for immediate compliance. The original letter briefly stated that after investigating the postage rates for domestic books, the current regulations have been revised and implemented since January of the ninth year of the Republic of China and have been in effect for ten years. At present, the level of social life is high and everything is expensive. The freight paid by post offices in various places has increased several times compared with the past, and the inland and remote areas are particularly expensive, which is far from what it was ten years ago. Post offices suffer heavy losses from the transshipment of books and newspapers, etc. The above-mentioned reasons have been carefully reviewed, and it is requested that the request to reduce postage be deemed difficult to implement. The department has reviewed the above-mentioned reasons and found that the situation is indeed true. Due to the previous order, the text has been written for reply.

In order to facilitate the work of the Central Research Institute, there is an organization of the Institute Affairs Conference, but because the site of the Central Institute has not yet been completed, the number of people attending the meeting is limited by the fact that the various research institutes are scattered in Beijing, Shanghai, and Ping. Jiading

Method for Seniority Pay Increase for Elementary School Teachers 87

The Jiading County Education Bureau held the fourth education administrative meeting on the 29th. The committee members attending were County Magistrate Chen, County Party Department representatives Gong Xianfu, Education Bureau Director Yang, Superintendent Yang, Pan Zhixing, Lu Shunxiang, Chen Baiyan, Zhou [unclear], Chen Zhangfu, and Liu. It was resolved that (1) Method for seniority pay increase for elementary school teachers and staff. Those who have continued to work in the county for three years will be given a one-level increase, those who have worked for six years will be given a two-level increase, those who have worked for eight to fourteen years will be given a one-level increase every two years, and those who have worked for fifteen to eighteen years will be given a one-level increase every year. Each level will be increased by 24 yuan per year. However, there is a maximum limit. The highest monthly salary for a central school principal is 65 yuan, the highest monthly salary for a central school director, a senior elementary school class teacher, and a full elementary school director is 45 yuan, the highest monthly salary for a single-level elementary school director is 42 yuan, the highest monthly salary for a junior elementary school director and class teacher, and a senior elementary school subject teacher is 40 yuan, the highest monthly salary for a junior elementary school subject teacher is 35 yuan, and other specific grade increases may still be increased outside the limit. (2) The budget for the 19th year is insufficient, and the construction costs for various elementary school buildings that will be built over the years will be temporarily suspended and will still be drawn from the reserve fund item at the end of the year for construction. (3) Stop running senior elementary school cram schools. (4) Promote the social education plan. Each central elementary school district in the county will set up a mass education center or a farmer education center. In addition to the existing ones, two more will be added this year. [unclear] will be omitted later. The retiring committee members signed and adjourned the meeting.

Senior High School 94

Make-up Examination Method Held at Wuben Girls' High School from August 11 The graduates of this year's senior high schools in Shanghai City were supervised and tested by the City Education Bureau. The test papers have been evaluated and published. However, some students who have not participated or whose grades are not up to standard are allowed to take make-up examinations. The following make-up examination methods are announced: (1) Students who have not participated in the supervised examination due to illness or special circumstances are allowed to take make-up examinations with proof from the school. (2) Those whose average score in the supervised examination subjects is below 1.5 should take make-up examinations for all subjects with D and E grades. (3) Those whose average score is above 1.5 but have two E grades should also take make-up examinations. (4) The grades of each subject in the make-up examination shall be calculated according to the original grading method. Those whose average score is above 1.5 shall be allowed to graduate. (5) Those whose average score is still below 1.5 after the make-up examination, or whose average score is above 1.5 but still have two E grades shall not be allowed to graduate. (6) Students who are still not allowed to graduate after the make-up examination shall study at the original school for half a year and shall be allowed to take another make-up examination during the summer vacation. (7) Those whose grades still do not meet the graduation standards after the second make-up examination shall not be allowed to take make-up examinations again, and the bureau shall issue a certificate of completion for the passing subjects. (8) Make-up examination dates: August 11 (Sunday) 8:30 a.m. to 11:30 a.m. Chinese Language 1:30 p.m. to 4:30 p.m. English Language August 12 (Tuesday) 8:30 a.m. to 11:30 a.m. Mathematics (9) Make-up examination location: Municipal Wuben Girls' High School, Huangjiaque Road, Ximen (10) Notice: (A) The test papers will be issued by the bureau. (B) Lunch will be prepared by the bureau. The cost of the meals shall be returned by each school. (C) Each student taking the make-up examination should prepare a recent 4.5-inch photo. Investigation of Memorial Weeks at Various Universities 96

According to Inspection Reports, Submitted to the Central Government for Correction (Guomin News Agency) The Training Department of the Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters of the Kuomintang stipulated early on that all political, military, police, and educational institutions should earnestly observe the weekly memorial service for Sun Yat-sen, the founding father of the Republic of China, to show respect. The various institutions, organizations, primary and secondary schools in the city have been urged and inspected repeatedly, and they have been able to comply. However, it is reported that some universities still do not pay much attention to the memorial week or make mistakes in the format. The department therefore sent personnel to various universities for inspection during several previous memorial weeks. The work has now been completed. According to statistics, the universities that do not hold memorial weeks include Aurora University and Fudan University. Those that hold them irregularly include Shanghai Private Business College, Sino-French Institute of Technology, and Xinmin University. Those with incorrect timing include Guanghua University (5:00 PM on Mondays), Great China University (2:00 PM on Sundays), and the Medical College of National Central University (1:00 PM on Wednesdays). Those with incorrect rituals include Guanghua University, Shanghai Law College, and East Asia University (all missing the singing of the Party song). It is reported that the department has submitted the inspection situation to the Central Training Department and forwarded it to the Education Bureau for supervision and correction.

Zhang Liquan Returns Home After Completing His Studies 103

Mr. Zhang Liquan, a native of Changshu, Jiangsu Province, went to the United States for further study at his own expense in 1925. He first studied economics at the University of Washington for two years, and then transferred to Indiana State University to study business administration, earning a Bachelor of Science in Business Administration. He returned to China a few days ago and will make a contribution to business administration in our country in the future.

Four Cases Resolved: (1) The remaining funds for participating in the Far Eastern Games will be deposited in the bank for future general use. Rockefeller unconditionally leased it to the association to promote amateur sports for six and a half years. During this period, Dr. Wang Zhengting and Mrs. Mei Huaquan repeatedly negotiated with Rockefeller to request a donation, but without success. The final contract expired on June 30th of this year, and it was not possible to extend it. Therefore, the association must seek another venue. World Olympics 110

Processing and Transforming the Large Sports Field, According to Los Angeles News, for the 10th Olympic Games to be held in 1932, the accommodation and transportation costs for athletes visiting from various European countries will only be $400 per person, due to special railway discounts and the convenience of building an Olympic Village to provide all facilities. As for neighboring Pacific countries, the costs are even lower. The large sports field in Los Angeles is being processed and transformed to accommodate 105,000 people. The nearby museum is being used for art competitions, and the armory is being used as a fencing arena. The swimming pool was originally planned to have a large grandstand built to accommodate 8,000 people. The large auditorium is currently used for wrestling performances and will also be used during the games. The waterway for speedboat competitions has been equipped with a 2,000-meter rowing course at the tip of Feiming outside the Port of Los Angeles. The Ross Sports Field in Arcadia will be used for modern pentathlon and equestrian performances. The Pasadena Rose Bowl (stadium) will be used as a football field. Japan Encourages Swimming

Preparing for the Next Olympics 111

Adding 50-Meter Backstroke and 100-Meter Backstroke, the Shanghai Swimming Championships for Middle Schools Will Be Held on August 16, (Special Correspondent in Japan) The All-Japan Student Swimming Federation held a general affairs meeting on the afternoon of the 26th. It was pointed out that the progress of both the backstroke and backstroke events is slower compared to others in the current situation. Since the 10th World Olympics will be held in the next year or two, it is necessary to plan and encourage methods to promote and revitalize these two events. It was decided to add the 50-meter backstroke and 100-meter backstroke to the inter-secondary school swimming competition of this year, for a total of fifteen events. These two events will also be added to the All-Japan Student Swimming Championships as new titles, which will be implemented from the next session to promote progress. The All-Japan Secondary School Swimming Championships are scheduled to be held on August 16th and 17th. The Kanto preliminaries are scheduled to be held on August 9th and 10th, both at the Meiji Jingu Grand Swimming Pool. Moreover, the lighting equipment for evening competitions has been nearly completed. Therefore, the aforementioned two competitions are planned to start at 5:30 PM or 6:00 PM, which will be the first open-air evening competition in Japan.

Executive and Supervisory Committee of the Advanced Business Association 115

Yesterday's Inauguration and Oath Taking, Election of Five Standing Committee Members, Xu Jiqing Elected Chairman. The entire Executive and Supervisory Committee of the Shanghai Advanced Business Association held an inauguration ceremony and mutually elected standing committee members and the chairman at 9 a.m. yesterday. Over a hundred representatives from various agencies and organizations attended. Details are recorded below:

Attendees: Zhao Jinqing and Shou Jingwei, representatives from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce; Jiang Huaisu, representative from the Shanghai Municipal Party Committee; Yu Hongjun, representative from the Municipal Government; Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau; Xiong Shihui, Commander of the Songhu Garrison; Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce; and guests Yu Qiaqing, Qin Runqing; and executive and supervisory committee members Xu Jiqing, Ye Huijun, Fang Jiaobo, Cheng Xiechun, Wen Lanting, Pei Yunqing, Yuan Ludeng, Ma Jiliang, Lu Fengzhu, Wang Xiaolai, Luo Qinghua, Lao Jingxiu, Chen Songyuan, Gu Xin'yi, Lu Qisheng, Wang Yansong, Zhu Wenqi, Wu Zhihao, Lu Wenshao, etc.

Meeting Agenda: (1) Ringing the bell to begin the meeting. (2) All committee members take their seats. (3) Publicly nominate a temporary chairman. (4) Bow three times to the Party and the national flag, and the portrait of Sun Yat-sen. (5) Reverently read Sun Yat-sen's will.

Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce Executive and Supervisory Committee Inauguration Photography (Wang Kai Photo)

(6) Three minutes of silence. (7) All executive and supervisory committee members take the oath of office. (8) Admonitory speech from the Party representative. (9) Admonitory speech from the Government representative. (10) Speech from the guest. (11) Chairman's reply. (12) Photo session and adjournment.

Meeting Proceedings: After the bell rang to start the meeting, guests and all committee members took their seats. Ye Huijun was publicly nominated as the temporary chairman. After the rituals, all executive and supervisory committee members stood solemnly to take the oath. Representatives from the Municipal Party Committee, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, the Municipal Government, the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, and guest Yu Qiaqing, etc., successively delivered speeches. Finally, the chairman gave a reply speech, and a photo session adjourned the meeting.

Oath of Office:

"We swear to accept the entrustment of all members of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce with utmost sincerity, abide by the charter, work hard to serve, not seek personal gain, and not be derelict in our duties. If we violate this oath, we are willing to accept the most severe sanctions from all members. We solemnly swear."

Admonitory Speech from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce: Minister of Industry and Commerce, Kong Xiangxi, could not attend in person and specially sent Mr. Zhao Jinqing to participate. Mr. Zhao stood up and read the admonitory speech, saying: "Shanghai is the center of the world's industry and commerce, and also the hub of economic development in East Asia. Therefore, it occupies an extremely important position in the national economy and international commerce. The mission of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce is therefore even greater. In terms of the national economy, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce is both the oldest chamber of commerce established in China and the first new chamber of commerce established in accordance with the new law. It cannot but bear the responsibility of guidance for the world's business community. At present, the problem of maintaining the world's established enterprises, the problem of gradually implementing industrial plans, and the problem of unemployment prevention and unemployment relief cannot be properly resolved without the sincere cooperation between the government and the business community. In terms of international commerce, commercial competition is becoming increasingly fierce. Foreign development cannot be achieved without concerted efforts and collective wisdom, nor can it be achieved by perfunctory actions and procrastination. Today, the executive and supervisory committee members of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce are sworn into office. Xiangxi deeply knows that you are all leaders in various industries. In the future, your planning and implementation will surely live up to expectations. However, I have always observed that the internal organization of important chambers of commerce in countries such as Britain, the United States, Germany, and Japan is extremely sound. Their investigation and statistics on domestic and foreign business conditions are also extremely detailed. Therefore, whether it is maintaining the domestic market or developing the foreign market, they can assist the government in actively implementing fundamental business plans. I especially hope to encourage you all." Zhao finished reading and continued to deliver a personal speech, briefly saying: "Gentlemen, just now Mr. Lu Fengzhu said that he wanted me to give an admonitory speech. The word 'admonitory speech' is of course appropriate for the government's position. I have been friends with you for many years and absolutely cannot give an admonitory speech, but I can only say to your association. However, what the Ministry of Industry and Commerce sent me to say today on behalf of it is not my tone, but the meaning of Minister Kong Yongzhi of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce. I have already drafted a manuscript and read it for you just now (see above). The above is the meaning of Minister Kong. I have a few more words to express and contribute to you. Let's look at the domestic situation. This kind of disturbance is nothing more than for the problem of livelihood, the problem of bread, the problem of rice bowls. In short, this problem is the problem of unemployment, which is very related to our commerce. To solve this unemployment problem, first of all, the production industry must be developed. The other day, when the Chamber of Commerce held a meeting of member representatives, I temporarily left the meeting due to business. Please Director Pan Gongzhan represent me. Director Pan's meaning is the same as my suggestion, which is to develop the production industry. But the most important thing at present is that everyone should promote domestic goods. I have heard the four words 'promote domestic goods' many times, but in fact, it has never taken effect. Especially those of us who are a little more noble are desperately using foreign goods. To reverse this trend, we still need our own leadership to enable the whole country

to use domestic goods, so that commerce can succeed and have a solid position. Therefore, developing the production industry starts with using domestic goods ourselves. Now our foreign trade is always heavily in surplus. Japan's total annual surplus is only three million. They already have a consistent idea from top to bottom that all clothing, food, and utensils must be made in their own country. Therefore, our most important task in the future is to promote domestic goods, which is to develop the production industry so that everyone in the country has food to eat. If everyone in the country has food to eat, the country will naturally be peaceful." After Zhao's speech, Shou Yicheng gave a speech, briefly saying: "Last summer, when I represented the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce to attend the International Chamber of Commerce, I conducted a detailed investigation on the organization and business of the chambers of commerce in London, Paris, Berlin, Hamburg, and other cities. I felt that their organization was far more complete than ours. I sought the reason for this, and the soundness of the organization of trade associations and the cooperation between experts, academic groups, and government agencies in various industries is their most powerful source. This time, the unified reorganization of Shanghai business groups has gone through many difficulties, which is probably what it should be in the process of reasonable chamber of commerce organization. However, the common disease of our country's society is often cooperation in name but not in reality. Fortunately, the committee members elected this time are all recommended by various industries and have a reputation for the times. Therefore, there must be full cooperation between the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the government, and between the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and various trade associations. I respectfully wish your association an immeasurable future development."

Admonitory Speech from the Municipal Party Committee: "Today is the day of the inauguration of all executive and supervisory committee members of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce. I feel that the decline of China's international status is largely due to the failure of industry and commerce to prosper. The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce occupies a very important position in the national industry and commerce and is the leader of the national merchants. After you take office today, I hope that you will lead the national merchants to revitalize industry and commerce. The mission of our party to complete the Chinese revolution is to have all Chinese people participate in the national revolution and jointly improve China's international status. Some people say that the people of all countries in the world who are oppressed in life are revolutionary, and the people who are not greatly oppressed in life are relatively non-revolutionary. Merchants are economically better than people from other sectors, so they are mostly non-revolutionary. Whether this statement is reasonable or not can be ignored, but Chinese merchants must not be compared with world merchants, because the Chinese nation is an oppressed nation, and Chinese merchants are also oppressed merchants. We must work hard to do the work of lifting oppression and improving China's international status. This is a point that we should pay attention to internationally. At present, the most difficult problem in the country is labor-capital disputes. Our party, whether it is for workers or merchants, wants to enable them to stand on an equal footing, so that our national organization can reach a very sound state. Therefore, we must figure out how to resolve labor-capital disputes in Shanghai so that they will not happen again, and gradually push them to the whole country so that everyone in all sectors of the country can reach an equal position, and then we can realize the national revolution. I think all of you committee members can pay attention to this point today."

Admonitory Speech from the Municipal Government: "Today is the day of the inauguration of the first committee of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce. I feel very honored to participate in the grand ceremony. In the past, the old-style Chamber of Commerce started in Shanghai, and today the new-style Chamber of Commerce also starts in Shanghai. The committee members present here are all leaders of the industrial and commercial circles in Shanghai, so this ceremony is a very valuable thing. The Chamber of Commerce is very related to the development of national industry and commerce, because the Chamber of Commerce is a collection of industrial and commercial leaders who can jointly study what should be developed and what should be reformed. Therefore, the development of national industry and commerce relies heavily on the Chamber of Commerce, but the former Chamber of Commerce failed to satisfy this point, because the former Chamber of Commerce was not unified or economical in organization, and the members did not represent industry and commerce, so it did not contribute much to industry and commerce. Some people say that the big problem of Chinese merchants is to talk about commerce in commerce. It seems to the brothers that talking about commerce in commerce is not the problem of Chinese merchants. The problem of Chinese merchants is that they cannot talk about commerce in commerce. In the past, the representatives of the Chamber of Commerce did not represent the interests of the whole, but represented the interests of a certain store or a certain individual. Of course, the organization was not good, but it was also impossible to talk about commerce in commerce, because talking about commerce in commerce is not an easy task. Without sufficient research, it is impossible to talk about it. Now the Chamber of Commerce is organized according to the central regulations, and the representatives are all leaders of various industries who can seek the interests of the whole. I hope that you can earnestly

talk about commerce in commerce in the future and fully study the methods of developing industry and commerce. The current unemployment problem is originally the responsibility of the government, but it cannot be solved without the joint cooperation of the government and merchants. We know that the unemployment problem is not a simple problem. The British government was overthrown because of the unemployment problem. At that time, it was thought that after the Labour Party organized the government, there might be considerable ways, but now this problem still cannot be solved. The situation in our China is certainly not exactly the same. This problem may be easier to solve. At present, the government has organized a committee to study the unemployment problem. Our merchants should pay full attention to it and cooperate with the government to carry it out. There will always be a day to solve this problem. Today, the committee members are certainly very important leaders in the industrial and commercial circles in Shanghai. I very much hope that you will cooperate with the government to seek the development of Chinese commerce and solve the problem of unemployment in China."

Speeches from Guests: (2) Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, delivered a congratulatory speech, saying: "East of the Yangtze River, west of the Pacific Ocean, there is Shanghai. Merchants gather, organizations are friendly, no one can match. Reorganize, unify, lead, and lift the outline. The first title of assuming office is to benefit and eliminate abuses, deeply united. Leading the merchants is the ladder for this. Sincerely dedicate congratulations, and the goods and materials will increase day by day." (2) Yu Qiaqing gave a speech, saying: "Today is the inauguration of all executive and supervisory committee members of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. I am very honored to participate in the grand meeting. Now, taking advantage of the presence of all representatives and committee members, I have a few words to say. First, I am not joining the Chamber of Commerce this time because I am old and busy, and I have been doing public affairs in Shanghai for 50 years. In recent years, my spirits have been poor, so I rarely participate in foreign affairs. There are various speculations from the outside world. I would like to explain to you that if there is anything you need me to do in the future, please do not decline. Second, the most painful thing for merchants at present is the problem of gold being expensive and silver being cheap (omitted). All committee members who are sworn into office today are leaders in various industries. I hope that you will pay attention to this issue." After the representatives and guests finished speaking one after another, the chairman gave a reply speech, and a photo session adjourned the meeting.

Election Situation: After the inauguration ceremony, the first executive committee meeting was held on the spot to elect standing committee members and the chairman, and to receive the handover of files from the Chamber of Commerce Reorganization Committee. Ye Huijun was still the temporary chairman. After the rituals, a vote was immediately held to elect the standing committee members. The elected were Xu Jiqing, Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, Yuan Ludeng, Ye Huijun, and other five people. Then, a vote was held to elect the chairman of the committee. As a result, Xu Jiqing was elected as chairman with eleven votes. After the announcement, Mr. Xu immediately went to the seat to request resignation. All committee members on the spot retained him. Representatives from the Party Committee, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, the Social Affairs Bureau, etc., repeatedly urged him not to resign. Then, the case of Executive Committee member Zhu Yinjiang's letter of resignation was discussed. It was decided to retain him and send a representative to persuade him. The meeting adjourned after a while.

New Chairman's Statement: After the new chairman, Mr. Xu Jiqing, was elected as chairman, he immediately requested resignation on the spot. A reporter from the Guowen News Agency visited Mr. Xu at the Zhejiang Industrial Bank yesterday afternoon. According to his conversation, he will definitely not take office as the chairman of this session. He said that in addition to submitting an oral resignation, a written resignation has also been submitted on the spot. No matter what, please the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to elect other capable people. The reporter asked, "What if the Chamber of Commerce does not allow the resignation?" Mr. Xu replied, "I will make further representations." It is also reported that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, because Chairman Xu does not agree to take office, will send Wang Yansong, Wang Xiaolai, and others to Mr. Xu's residence to earnestly retain him.

Yu Qiaqing and others Enjoy a Banquet This Afternoon: Giants of the business community, Yu Qiaqing and Qin Runqing, etc., were very happy that the new chairman and standing committee members have been elected. Deduction of Education Fee Receipt Fee and Collection Fee

Effective July 1st of This Year

The Shanghai Special City Land Bureau issued real estate deeds in accordance with Article 7 of the Shanghai Special City Real Estate Deed Regulations, charging 5 jiao per sheet. Therefore, according to the old regulations, 5 jiao of silver is still collected for each deed, and another 3 jiao for education fees and 1 fen for receipt fees are collected, totaling 8 jiao and 1 fen per sheet. The bureau believes that the rules for the real estate transfer tax are now presented to the municipal government for approval and promulgation, and the municipal expenses collected as an attachment have also been presented for approval to uniformly collect 5%. The deed tax and surcharges referred to in Article 8 of the deed issuance regulations all have new regulations. The 3 jiao for education fees and 1 fen for receipt fees that have always been collected on each deed according to the old regulations should be cancelled. A special request has been made to the municipal government for approval, effective July 1st of this year, to collect 5 jiao of silver per deed according to the regulations. Shanghai County
