Survey: Japan's Trade Sluggish in the First Half of the Year 206

Dentsu, Tokyo: The estimated total amount of foreign trade through 27 ports nationwide in the first half of Showa 5 (1930) is as follows (unit: 1,000 yen): Exports: 729,794; Imports: 947,592; Total: 1,677,386; Trade deficit: 217,788. Compared to the first half of last year, exports decreased by 28% and imports decreased by 26%. Regarding important commodities, Japan's largest export commodity is raw silk, but in the first half of this year, only 172,774,000 yen were exported, a sharp decrease of 176,839,000 yen compared to 349,613,000 yen in the same period last year, falling to less than half. Next, the export amount of cotton fabrics was 149,887,000 yen, and the export amount of silk fabrics was 55,180,000 yen, both with considerable decreases. The import amount of cotton, a major import commodity, was 260,708,000 yen, also a decrease of 69,302,000 yen. Based on this calculation, the total trade deficit for the first half of the year, including trade with colonies, was 270 million yen. The reasons for this trade slump are: 1. The fall in silver prices has greatly affected trade with China; 2. The sharp decline in U.S. raw silk consumption.

Japan's Cash Outflow in the First Half of the Year 207

Dentsu, Tokyo: According to the Bank of Japan's announcement, the amount of cash outflow since the lifting of the gold export ban until the end of the first half of this year was 225 million yen. In addition, the amount of cash withdrawn from the Bank of Japan and scattered among the general public without flowing out of the country also reached 5 million yen.

Recent Trends in German Drama, by Manhua 210

The German theater scene has shown distinctive changes in the last two months.

Now that spring has passed and summer has arrived, German drama is blooming with vibrant flowers. Many great plays have been performed one by one. Although there have been no amazing achievements, on average, there has been an opportunity for every German citizen to appreciate theatrical art. Half of this is due to the development of theatrical troupes, but the efforts of directors and actors cannot be ignored. As for the audience, it seems that there is a kind of preference, and this preference is the motivation for creating the current situation. They all like to study social, personal, and even political problems from the plays, thinking about what they reflect and what their meaning is. But strictly speaking, a play does not necessarily have to clearly solve a problem for you. If that were the case, it would become a paper solving problems, not a problem play. The so-called problem play uses sufficient force in the play to express a problem. The solution is either implied or left to the audience to think about with their own brains. There is no doubt that German audiences welcome plays about social and political problems, such as anti-Semitism, the drinking club movement, the ban on drugs, birth control, and the improvement of prisoner treatment. These are all the themes of the plays that have been popular in Berlin theaters in the spring and summer. Although the involvement is extensive, the result is successful. "Journey's End," which caused a sensation in the British literary world, has a German translation. It is considered one of the best war works of the year, but after the performance, it does not seem to have been a great success. As for the abolition of the death penalty, it has attracted a lot of attention in modern Germany, because the public has discovered many judicial errors. Langha Fulanck's "Ursache" discusses the abolition of the death penalty and advocates amending the current criminal law. Also, Wang Erfu's "Cyankali" and Kreide's "Article 218" have made considerable contributions to this issue. These two plays are not only suitable for stage application, but also have great achievements in directing and performance. Therefore, audiences are most satisfied with the selection of these two plays. In addition, Ficklinburg's "Amnesty" attracted many viewers to the Fuchsborn Theater with its brave attitude and detached thinking. Riefeqia Hawthorne's "Dreyfus's Miserable Memories" is a great tragedy against traditional thinking. Not only was the audience satisfied, but even the Berlin newspapers were full of praise, especially for the better criticism of Emile Zola, the protagonist who went to Dreyfus. Among many complicated issues, political concepts are the most profound. In the near future, it is expected that many plays on political issues will be produced. The most eye-catching is the play called "1914." The author of this play is called George William Mauchin. We don't care who Mauchin is; his name is always heard for the first time. But the fact is not so. Mauchin is the pseudonym of Emile Ludwig. As soon as Ludwig is mentioned, almost all Easterners know him. He is an authoritative figure in the German literary world. It is said that after the premiere of this "July 1914" in Berlin, other cities will perform it in order. Recently, there is a special phenomenon that was not seen in Berlin before, that is, the rejection of works by foreign writers. In the past two years, German theaters almost exclusively performed famous foreign plays. According to the statistics of one week in the German theater advertisements two years ago, there were three types of Shaw, two types of Wilde, and two types of Shakespeare. There was one of Galsworthy and five French comedies. At that time, German works were extremely pitiful and almost had no status. But now, times have changed. Depending on the natural trend, the result must not be intentional, and foreign works have gradually been rejected. Shaw's works are the only remaining ones, and there are only a few comedies popular in Paris.

Dutch Beauty Queen Deposed 211

The God of Beauty Comes from Herself. Add to the Garden.

She probably isn't qualified for beauty pageants anymore. This isn't just empty talk. You only have to look at the recent deposition of Dutch beauty queen Emmy Kuster to prove it. After she was selected, she was disqualified due to her age and marital status. But although she encountered misfortune and reigned for a very short time, this matter instead made her gain more admirers and exposed the naivety and ridiculousness of modern beauty pageants. After carefully inspecting many participating beauties, the judges in The Hague, the capital of the Netherlands, unanimously elected Emmy Kuster as Miss Netherlands and sent her to represent the Netherlands at the Miss World pageant held in America. There is no doubt that Ms. Emmy did possess the talent and appearance that a Dutch beauty should have, so after she was elected, the Dutch people congratulated her, believing that her beauty was enough to compete with beauties from any country without shame. But the unfortunate thing happened here. Because of her fame, everyone was naturally eager to know her family and living conditions. Unexpectedly, an investigation revealed that she was already thirty years old, had been married for eleven years, and had a nine-year-old daughter. So, a group of judges immediately reconvened and decided to depose her and add the title of Miss Netherlands to Ms. Mile Rie Vande Rese, who was originally the runner-up. Their reason was that the rules of the beauty pageant stipulate that only unmarried women under the age of twenty-five are allowed to participate, as if they thought that Ms. Emmy would never be beautiful due to her children and age. But unfortunately, it was still they themselves who chose Ms. Emmy as the most beautiful woman in the Netherlands. Why can't a married woman, and especially a glorious mother, be considered beautiful or even be excluded from the competition? This can be asked of Clement Vautel, the famous satirist of the Paris News. Below are his words:

"At the wedding feast on Mount Ida, when the gods were vying for the apple of beauty, the two most powerful competitors were both married. Juno was married to Jupiter, and Venus was married to Vulcan. She had also given birth to Cupid. If the rules at that time were the same as now, another competitor, Minerva, could have said to Paris, the judge, that they were married women and should be removed, and only I am a virgin, quickly give me the apple of beauty. But she didn't say it at the time, so Venus won after all. In my opinion, the only thing that matters in a beauty pageant is beauty. Marriage or childbirth doesn't matter. Open your eyes and you can see how many weak, thin, or even ugly women become beautiful and good-looking after they get married, get sexually satisfied, or become mothers. This kind of happy change is common, so how can we forbid them from joining? Especially in today's relaxed sexual relations, how can we recognize marriage as the decline of beauty and childbirth as the end of beauty? Is their restriction consistent with aesthetic viewpoints? In my personal opinion, thirty years old is the time when a woman is truly beautiful, not the beauty of hope, but the beauty of reality. The dismissal of the Dutch woman, in my opinion, is not only unfair, but also violates the good intentions of mankind." Vautel also said that this beauty pageant is an international competition, and the deposed Dutch woman might as well sue in the International Court, which is right next to her in The Hague.

Smart readers, what is your opinion? (Junshan) Painting by Ms. Jin Qijing

Special Article 215

Hudson Factory Owner's Record After Visiting the *Crow* Automobile Exhibition

The Grandest Event in the United States

The 1930 American Automobile Exhibition was a hundred times more lively and magnificent than in previous years. The automobiles displayed by each factory were the latest, most magnificent, strongest, and most unique vehicles of 1930. The progress of modern mechanical science is so ingenious and rapid that it is worthy of praise.

This year's exhibition not only shows that the automobile industry is a source of wealth for American finances, but also a driving force for the development of everything. The factories joining the association have a total of 4.5 million workers, a total capital of 40 billion U.S. dollars, and are the largest factories that use the most steel, copper, lead, coal, wood, leather, velvet fabrics, glass, and paint.

A Billion-Dollar Business

This great automobile industry contains billions of dollars in costs. People across the country have a stake in it and should bear a share of the responsibility. This huge amount of commercial development increases profits tenfold without limit. At the end of each month, the country's finances are always affected, and even countries around the world are amazed.

Today, 15 million Americans rely on the automobile industry for their livelihood. These people are the highest paid and most well-treated. There are approximately 25 million vehicles traveling across the country every day. The value of automobiles produced each year is approximately 40 billion gold dollars. The value of spare parts and miscellaneous items already in use is over 65 billion yuan. In 1929, automobile taxes totaled 925 million gold dollars, which is staggering. Twenty states across the country have automobile manufacturing plants or assembly plants. Last year, 37 states opened 7,500 automobile branch plants.

Developing Other Businesses

The automobile industry has developed, and the gasoline and rubber industries have also increased sharply as a result. The railway transportation industry has also greatly developed. Statistics show that more than 3.5 million freight cars are used to transport automobiles each year. More than 3 million people are employed to manage car affairs. From the above numbers and the large amount of raw materials and great manpower, it can be seen that the automobile industry is indeed the largest in scale among various industries. Huge amounts of money are spent on research and improvement to ensure that car owners enjoy full benefits. The development of automobiles is changing with each passing day and can be said to have reached its peak.

Unprecedented Exhibition

New styles and increased colors. This year's automobile exhibition is truly unprecedented. The revitalization of the automobile industry is of great significance to the saving of time and space, the increase of its function and capacity, the development of domestic business, and the happiness of society. Today, the position occupied by automobiles has become a central object, and the revitalization of everything depends on it.

8 Million Workers Include One-Third of the Country's Population. No other event in the world is more grand than this. This year's automobile exhibition meets the interests of the people, promotes the progress of business, adapts to the trends of the world, and provides for the needs of society. It can be called the supreme event in the United States and an unprecedented exhibition in the world.

The International Automobile Championship - Ji Ren 216

One Hundred and Fifty Cars Competing - Nashi Declared the Winner

The annual International Automobile Championship held in France took place this spring at the Leme Racecourse. A total of 150 cars participated. Nashi's car emerged victorious, demonstrating not only superior speed but also exceptional mechanical endurance. The George Ham's gold medal was awarded publicly, along with a championship flag for commemoration. Nashi's car factory received an avalanche of congratulatory telegrams from various countries, making its name a sensation in Europe and America. Nashi "400" secured the leading title in the international automobile realm. Nashi's unexpected victory in the 5,000-kilometer championship was attributed to the lack of prior preparation or testing. The factory randomly selected two cars for the competition: a dual large-cylinder car driven by Mr. Luo Wen and a dual large eight-cylinder car driven by Mr. Tu Mu. In the end, Mr. Tu's car scored the highest and performed the best. Despite the intense and challenging competition, Nashi's car suffered no damage. Nashi "400" ultimately won the international championship and broke a world record.

The speed of Tu Mu's Nashi dual large eight-cylinder car averaged 100 kilometers per hour this year, with a top speed of 138 kilometers per hour. While speed is important in this competition, agility, ease of operation, convenient control, and road safety are also key judging criteria. The French Automobile Spring Race is the most enthusiastic competition in the world, with historical value, emotional significance, and mechanical testing. It originated from the earlier Glidden Tour and the Pikes Peak Hill Climb. This year's race started from Porte Maillot in Paris and ended at Le Havre and Lille, covering a total of 5,000 kilometers over eight days, involving various tests of mountain climbing, air conditioning, braking, and speed, with excellent results.

Temporary care stations were set up along the final race route, with personnel patrolling and monitoring the cars' movements day and night. Notaries accompanied the cars to record the drivers' skills and the cars' performance. Mechanics and judges were on hand to inspect and score various situations, such as increased heat during uphill climbs, valve damage, driver fatigue, and uncomfortable seating.

Each time a race car arrived at a station, it was put on display for the audience to view and to solicit opinions from visitors for public judgment. Remarkably, everyone praised Nashi cars as the most magnificent and robust among all the cars. Its swift and steady performance on rural roads and fields, and its exceptional durability, truly made it a leader among automobiles. Since this competition, Nashi's reputation in France has grown day by day, and people's confidence in it has deepened. The number of managers and distributors has greatly increased, and sales have also suddenly increased tenfold. According to news reporters who participated in monitoring the competition, Nashi never encountered any obstacles along the difficult journey and maintained smooth and perfect performance from beginning to end. During an air conditioning test in the city of Blois, the weather was rainy and cold that night, but the Nashi car was able to travel ten kilometers in five seconds comfortably and steadily. Nashi "400" is indeed the most ideal car for all-weather travel.

Neither of the two Nashi cars that participated were custom-made. The dual-spark six-cylinder car driven by Mr. Luo Wen was randomly selected from a large batch of cars shipped directly from the American headquarters to France. The dual-spark eight-cylinder car driven by Mr. Tu Mu was selected from the local management office's showroom. It is truly remarkable that these two cars were entered into this intense competition and won the championship among 150 carefully selected and finely crafted automobiles, and that their bodies remained strong throughout. It is therefore not surprising that Nashi cars are praised and trusted by Europeans and Americans alike. Do not rank at the top.

Automotive Manufacturing Industry Growth - Lin 217

Small Cars Sell Well

The British automobile market showed signs of progress in 1929. According to "Motor Trade" magazine, the total number of cars of various styles manufactured in Britain that year was 180,426, valued at £44,945,918. In terms of both quantity and value, this represents a significant increase compared to previous years. The previous year's car production was 154,495 units, valued at £38,763,946, but car production in 1928 was lower than in 1927, which saw a total of 161,920 cars manufactured, valued at £43,550,561. However, this was only a temporary deviation, as the automobile industry has been growing and developing since 1922. In that year, only 38,000 cars were manufactured, valued at £20,500,000. In eight years, the number of cars manufactured has increased fivefold. However, the value has only increased by slightly more than double, which is due to the decrease in car prices and the popularity of smaller cars, which are also less expensive. Regarding the production of small cars, there have been many changes. Twelve-horsepower cars used to dominate the automotive industry, and their sales often topped the charts due to their popularity. However, according to the breakdown of various car production figures in 1929, many changes have been observed. The number of ten-horsepower and below cars was no less than 73,289, accounting for more than half of the total. The speed of its development can be seen from the production figures for 1928 and 1927, which were 50,586 and 38,992 respectively. Last year, the number of twelve-horsepower cars was 45,364. A comparison with the production figures for twelve-horsepower cars in 1928 and 1927 reveals a significant change, with 51,915 in 1928 and 69,996 in 1927. The second most outstanding car was the six-horsepower, with 24,758 units produced last year, 12,398 in 1928, and only 11,220 in 1927. The total number of the above-mentioned ten-horsepower and below, twelve-horsepower, and sixteen-horsepower cars was 143,411 last year. The production volume of various cars

Page 26

The total number is 180,426 units. The magnitude of the demand can be imagined. The changes and the increase in the first two items and the decline in the third item are quite interesting. The growth of small cars is due to the popularity of seven-horsepower and eight-horsepower cars. These cars are the cheapest and have low running costs, and they run smoothly. The sixteen-horsepower car occupies an outstanding position because experienced drivers all want to switch to larger horsepower. The characteristic of the sixteen-horsepower is that the engine power is increased, while the price is not very different from that of small models. In short, this car is the best of the cars and the price has a certain standard. The reason for the lower sales of twelve-horsepower cars may be due to the change to larger horsepower. The twelve-horsepower car can be called a large-scale production compared to other cars made in Britain. There are often two or three factories that produce large quantities, all built according to their respective models. However, this is a reproduction of work, so its appearance is often similar. In this situation, the independent nature is often reduced, and British car drivers regard the car's inability to be unique and novel as wrong.

The above statistics do not include Ford's production. The mutual connection of British car manufacturers is also being heard more and more. In recent years, the names of several famous factories have disappeared from the list of car manufacturers. The difficult situation of small manufacturers has not been eliminated. For example, out of the total of 10,426 cars last year, 160,000 cars were manufactured by nine factories, and 140,000 of these 160,000 cars came from five factories.

Long-Distance Buses in Guangzhou Special Municipality - Huang Lang 218

The Guangzhou Special Municipality has a vast area and frequent transportation, making it easier to carry out road construction compared to Shanghai, where the concessions have limited the extent of development. With the recent opening of roads, the flow of merchants has become more convenient. The most important benefit of transportation is naturally public buses, but the regulations are strict and restrictions are tight. Here is a summary of recent news:

Regulations on Bus Operating Hours: It has been decided by the municipal government's administrative meeting to extend the operating hours of long-distance passenger buses by two hours, from 6:00 AM to 12:00 AM daily, to facilitate transportation. The Public Utilities Bureau has been instructed to notify all companies to comply.

Designated Bus Routes: As Guangzhou's roads are being opened up and bus traffic is increasing, accidents often occur due to speeding. To maintain public safety and eliminate danger, it is planned to build pedestrian routes, each 20 feet in diameter, with stone along the edges of easy-to-walk channels at intersections and T-junctions on various roads. Pedestrians must cross the road within the lines. Traffic will be directed by the police at turning points on each road, and red lights will be installed at turning lines, similar to Shanghai. In addition, white wooden signs will be erected on suburban roads where there is no lighting at night. All of these measures are designed to facilitate traffic and avoid danger.

Buses Must Not Arbitrarily Display Advertisements: All advertisements inside and outside long-distance passenger buses must not be posted arbitrarily to avoid obstructing the view. Recently, many advertisements have been posted inside the buses, covering the stop schedules, and the Public Utilities Bureau has strictly ordered them to be removed.

Painting and Repairing Buses: The vehicles and components of long-distance passenger buses should be repaired immediately and the bodies repainted. Repairs should be completed within this year so that the buses can be driven to the Public Utilities Bureau for inspection and renewal of licenses, to enhance the appearance.

Circle-City Buses Now in Operation: The municipal government has decided to operate circle-city long-distance buses to facilitate travel for residents around the city. It has purchased four municipal buses from Hong Kong. To test the speed and reliability of the buses, the municipal government conducted a trial run on the 23rd of last month, driving the buses around the city for an actual test. The buses have fourteen seats, with white paint on the upper part of the exterior and green paint on the lower part. Both sides have the city emblem, which is very beautiful. They have recently been put into operation to benefit travelers. The route has a total of six stops, each charging eight copper coins. The route starts from the West Gate to the Provincial Government, which is one stop. From Yuehua Road to Panyu County, which is the second stop. From Panyu County, Dadongmen, Xiaodongmen is one stop. From Xiaodongmen to Guolan Street is the third stop. From Weixin Road Intersection to Pujiao Bridge is the fourth stop. From Pujiao Bridge to West Gate is one stop. All the citizens praise the convenience.

Changing the Names of Bus Routes: The Public Utilities Bureau has named the Guangzhou long-distance bus routes with the three colors of red, yellow, and green to distinguish them. Now, as the number of roads increases, the names of the routes should be redefined. The original yellow route, which was divided into three stops, is now changed to the first route, the second route, and the third route. The red bus is changed to the fourth route, and the original green route is changed to the fifth route. Recently, the sixth route, the eighth route, the ninth route, the tenth route, the eleventh route, and the twelfth route have been newly opened. In the future, new routes will be named according to these numbers to facilitate distinction and memorization. The proposal has been submitted to the Municipal Council for approval and has been ordered to be implemented.

Banning Special License Plates: The municipal government believes that five buses should be opened first on the Dongmen to Shahe route to facilitate transportation. The special license plates previously issued by the Dong'an Company, which is contracted to operate the Dongshen Road bus route from the Cangbian Road intersection to Shahe, and all rotten "wild chicken car" license plates will be collected and revoked and not allowed to operate on that route.
